	c_excludes  ->  SYM_EXCLUDE assertions .   (rule 65)
	assertions  ->  assertions . assertion   (rule 67)

	boolean_literal  ->  . SYM_FALSE   (rule 93)

	real_value  ->  . '-' V_REAL   (rule 224)
